SELECT "a"."Id", "a"."FirstName", "a"."LastName", "a"."Address", "a"."PhoneNumber", "t"."UserId", "t"."RoleId", "t"."Id", "t"."ConcurrencyStamp", "t"."Name", "t"."NormalizedName", "a"."DateCreated", "a"."DateUpdated"
FROM "AspNetUsers" AS "a"
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT "a0"."UserId", "a0"."RoleId", "a1"."Id", "a1"."ConcurrencyStamp", "a1"."Name", "a1"."NormalizedName"
    FROM "AspNetUserRoles" AS "a0"
    INNER JOIN "AspNetRoles" AS "a1" ON "a0"."RoleId" = "a1"."Id"
) AS "t" ON "a"."Id" = "t"."UserId"
ORDER BY "a"."Id", "t"."UserId", "t"."RoleId"
